Are birthlessness, peace, and the absence of attributes.
The supreme leaders, the buddhas, have these strengths and retentions,
And the strength of the ten strengths. {18}
{{milestone:{label:30.24,id:UT22084-055-001-2743}}}“ ‘The supreme good qualities, the accumulation of qualities,
Are the supreme qualities, wisdom, retentions, strengths,
The supreme manifestation of miraculous powers,
And the attainment of the five{{note:{index967,id:UT22084-055-001-2744}}} supreme higher cognitions. {19}
{{milestone:{label:30.25,id:UT22084-055-001-2745}}}“ ‘There is no essence here to be known whatsoever.
There is no coming, no going; that is the subtle{{note:{index968,id:UT22084-055-001-2746}}} mode of phenomena.{{note:{index969,id:UT22084-055-001-2747}}}
The essence of phenomena has no movement whatsoever,
Thus the mode of phenomena is the mode of no movement. {20}
{{milestone:{label:30.26,id:UT22084-055-001-2748}}}“ ‘The natural mode is not in the accumulation of words. 
This mode, this nature, does not dwell anywhere. {{page:{number:191,id:UT22084-055-001-6024,folio:F.96.b}}}
The natural mode is without dwelling, is nondependent.
It is the level of peace, the stainless domain of the jinas. {21}
{{milestone:{label:30.27,id:UT22084-055-001-2749}}}“ ‘It is the mode of peace, complete peace, total peace.
That mode does not dwell anywhere. 
It always accompanies the nature of things.
It is subtle,{{note:{index970,id:UT22084-055-001-2750}}} difficult to see, and an unfluctuating state. {22}
{{milestone:{label:30.28,id:UT22084-055-001-2751}}}“ ‘It does not fluctuate but continues to be itself. 
It is a continuing nature that neither stays nor comes.
This continuing nature cannot be described. 
It is the empty, unfluctuating continuity of phenomena. {23}
{{milestone:{label:30.29,id:UT22084-055-001-2752}}}“ ‘It is taught in words but it is not the mode of words.
The mode of the nature of words is the mode of phenomena.
The aggregation of words has no location anywhere,
And that mode of its nature is the mode of phenomena. {24}
{{milestone:{label:30.30,id:UT22084-055-001-2753}}}“ ‘The words that describe the mode are not the mode of being.
The nature of phenomena is a mode of subtle{{note:{index971,id:UT22084-055-001-2754}}} meaning.
Though words are spoken, that is not the mode of being;
Words cannot be found and neither can the mode of being. {25}
{{milestone:{label:30.31,id:UT22084-055-001-2755}}}“ ‘There is no endlessness, nor an end, nor a mode in between. 
There is no existence nor nonexistence, nor a partial mode.
The knowledge of that mode of nature
Is the same in the teachings of all the supreme jinas. {26}
{{milestone:{label:30.32,id:UT22084-055-001-2756}}}“ ‘The stainless, pure, ultimate state—
Peace, complete peace, without stain, free of stain—
There are no concepts or pride in the state of peace
That is taught by the Jina, the one with perfect compassion. {27}
{{milestone:{label:30.33,id:UT22084-055-001-2757}}}“ ‘In this there is no usage of letters.
It is a vast mode, a vast mode of meaning.
The buddhas honor it; the jinas praise it.
The appearance of the Dharma is a subtle mode. {28}
{{milestone:{label:30.34,id:UT22084-055-001-2758}}}“ ‘The unequaled sugatas remain in that 
Stainless, vast treasure of the Dharma.
They teach the stainless, precious Dharma, 
The ultimate truth of emptiness, the subtle{{note:{index972,id:UT22084-055-001-2759}}} mode of meaning.’ {{note:{index973,id:UT22084-055-001-2760}}} {29}
{{milestone:{label:30.35,id:UT22084-055-001-2761}}}“When King Dṛdhadatta heard
That the supreme human was teaching this samādhi,
He then{{note:{index974,id:UT22084-055-001-2762}}} came into the presence of the compassionate Jina 
Accompanied by eighty quintillion others. {30}
{{milestone:{label:30.36,id:UT22084-055-001-2763}}}“The sovereign over men felt veneration for the Jina
Who was endowed with the strengths, and bowed down to his feet.
While he stayed in front of the one with the ten strengths,
Filled with joy, he placed his ten fingers together in homage. {31}
{{milestone:{label:30.37,id:UT22084-055-001-2764}}}“The Jina, who was perfect, with control over his senses,
Perceived the king’s pure conduct. {{page:{number:192,id:UT22084-055-001-6025,folio:F.97.a}}}
The supreme human knew his aspiration
And taught him this supreme samādhi. {32}
{{milestone:{label:30.38,id:UT22084-055-001-2765}}}“When the king had heard this ultimate truth
He experienced a vast, superior joy.
He gave up all of the four continents.
He abandoned pleasures and left his home. {33}
{{milestone:{label:30.39,id:UT22084-055-001-2766}}}“When the king gave up the world and entered homelessness
For the sake of enlightenment and to become a jina,
All the people in this Jambudvīpa{{note:{index975,id:UT22084-055-001-2767}}}
Gave up all sensory pleasures and entered homelessness too. {34}
{{milestone:{label:30.40,id:UT22084-055-001-2768}}}“At that time there was a vast assembly with the ten strengths.
There were many diligent bhikṣus and bhikṣuṇīs.
At that time, herbs grew without ploughing, 
And devas came to serve and attend to them. {35}
{{milestone:{label:30.41,id:UT22084-055-001-2769}}}“The three orange Dharma robes manifested,
Perfectly cut and sewn, without parallel,
Unsullied, stainless, adorned, beautifully golden,
Arising from the Buddha’s qualities and the power of merit. {36}
{{milestone:{label:30.42,id:UT22084-055-001-2770}}}“See, young man, look how that supreme king 
Gave up the entire world and entered homelessness.{{note:{index976,id:UT22084-055-001-2771}}}
In the age of destruction there will be many beings
Who will have few possessions but will not leave their homes.{{note:{index977,id:UT22084-055-001-2772}}} {37}
{{milestone:{label:30.43,id:UT22084-055-001-2773}}}“There will be many in chains and suffering punishments,
Who are abused, threatened, and have unwished-for suffering.
There will be many who will have to endure harm from royal families,{{note:{index978,id:UT22084-055-001-2774}}}
Who will have very few possessions and no food in their homes. {38}
{{milestone:{label:30.44,id:UT22084-055-001-2775}}}“They will have very short lives and no wealth.
They will be very careless and have no power of merit.
They will be stupid, and unskilled in any craft.
They will be in poverty with nothing in their homes. {39}
{{milestone:{label:30.45,id:UT22084-055-001-2776}}}“They will be impure and desire the wives of others.
They will be envious and extremely rash.
They will be degenerate and behave badly—
Yet they will say, ‘I am going to be a buddha.’{{note:{index979,id:UT22084-055-001-2777}}} {40}
{{milestone:{label:30.46,id:UT22084-055-001-2778}}}“They will make deceptive promises and be brazen, saying,
‘I am wealthy and I will give the wealth of the Dharma to the world.’{{note:{index980,id:UT22084-055-001-2779}}}
They will cause harm, be hypocritical and dishonest—
Yet they will say, ‘I am going to be a buddha.’ {41}
{{milestone:{label:30.47,id:UT22084-055-001-2780}}}“They will delight in killing, binding, and attacking others;
They will have bad conduct, and be cruel and aggressive.
They will have no gratitude, be divisive and violent— {{page:{number:193,id:UT22084-055-001-6026,folio:F.97.b}}}
Yet will say, ‘I am a noble practitioner of bodhisattva conduct.’ {42}
{{milestone:{label:30.48,id:UT22084-055-001-2781}}}“They will become angry with anyone 
Who they hear teaching bodhisattva conduct.
When they hear something that is stupid{{note:{index981,id:UT22084-055-001-2782}}} and mistaken 
They will repeat those blameworthy words a hundred times.{{note:{index982,id:UT22084-055-001-2783}}} {43}
{{milestone:{label:30.49,id:UT22084-055-001-2784}}}“Young man, having heard these words of mine,
Do not follow{{note:{index983,id:UT22084-055-001-2785}}} those others.
If you wish to reach the highest enlightenment
They are not to be trusted, even in a dream. {44}
{{milestone:{label:30.50,id:UT22084-055-001-2786}}}“One could recount for hundreds of eons the many qualities
Ascribed to the austere disciplines of mendicancy,
But without possessing those qualities
One will not attain the peace of the highest enlightenment. {45}
{{milestone:{label:30.51,id:UT22084-055-001-2787}}}“Always be good and gentle.
Always have pure conduct and a serene mind.
Continually maintain pure conduct,
And before long you will attain the supreme samādhi. {46}
{{milestone:{label:30.52,id:UT22084-055-001-2788}}}“Do not be proud and do not be harsh.
Always have a mind that is serene.
Eliminate all pride, arrogance, and hiding of your faults,
And attain this supreme samādhi. {47}
{{milestone:{label:30.53,id:UT22084-055-001-2789}}}“Always remember the Jina’s qualities.
The color of perfect gold, shining brightly,
Like the sky at night filled with stars:
The Sage’s body is filled with signs. {48}
{{milestone:{label:30.54,id:UT22084-055-001-2790}}}“The descendant of Manu who remembers the moon of the Sage 
While walking, sitting, standing, or lying down
Will always have the Teacher present before him,
And he will have vast happiness.{{note:{index984,id:UT22084-055-001-2791}}} {i}
{{milestone:{label:30.55,id:UT22084-055-001-2792}}}“Holding many powders and ointments,
And excellent parasols, banners, canopies, and flags,
Always make offerings to the Sugata
And this supreme samādhi will soon be attained. {49}
{{milestone:{label:30.56,id:UT22084-055-001-2793}}}“Holding many musical instruments
And excellent, exquisite{{note:{index985,id:UT22084-055-001-2794}}} incense, garlands, and flowers,
Make offerings always to the Jina’s stūpas
And this supreme samādhi will soon be attained. {50}
{{milestone:{label:30.57,id:UT22084-055-001-2795}}}“With many kinds of excellent songs and dance,
With amusements and performances made with a pure mind,
With excellent lights and incense, 
Always make excellent offerings to the unequaled one.{{note:{index986,id:UT22084-055-001-2796}}} {i}
{{milestone:{label:30.58,id:UT22084-055-001-2797}}}“With hundreds of paṇava drums and loud mṛdaṅga drums,
With paṭaha drums, lutes,{{note:{index987,id:UT22084-055-001-2798}}} the excellent sound of flutes, {{page:{number:194,id:UT22084-055-001-6027,folio:F.98.a}}}
With the qualities of music of various kinds of melodious sounds, 
Make an offering to the Guide with a pure mind. {51}
{{milestone:{label:30.59,id:UT22084-055-001-2799}}}“Create beautiful images of the Buddha,
Perfectly made of precious materials,{{note:{index988,id:UT22084-055-001-2800}}}
That are attractive and extremely beautiful,
And this supreme samādhi will soon be attained. {52}
{{milestone:{label:30.60,id:UT22084-055-001-2801}}}“Make excellent images that are fashioned 
From gold or silver, and also sandalwood,
That are attractive and extremely beautiful,
And this supreme samādhi will soon be attained.{{note:{index989,id:UT22084-055-001-2802}}} {i}
{{milestone:{label:30.61,id:UT22084-055-001-2803}}}“Make images that are fashioned of clay,
Or stone, or wood, or painted,
That are attractive and extremely beautiful, 
And this supreme samādhi will soon be attained.{{note:{index990,id:UT22084-055-001-2804}}} {ii}
{{milestone:{label:30.62,id:UT22084-055-001-2805}}}“Always remain in the solitude of forests,
Forsaking the joys of villages and towns.
Be without a companion, like a rhinoceros,
And this supreme samādhi will soon be attained. {53}
{{milestone:{label:30.63,id:UT22084-055-001-2806}}}“I am the Lord of the Dharma; you are my son.
Train in this samādhi practice of mine.
I was at that time Dṛdhadatta, the world-renowned
Ruler over the descendants of Manu.{{note:{index991,id:UT22084-055-001-2807}}} {54}
{{milestone:{label:30.64,id:UT22084-055-001-2808}}}“Seeking this peace, this supreme samādhi, 
I made offerings to countless buddhas in the past.
I always maintained pure conduct
And I honored those with the ten strengths.{{note:{index992,id:UT22084-055-001-2809}}} {55}
{{milestone:{label:30.65,id:UT22084-055-001-2810}}}“Seeking this peace, this supreme samādhi,
In the past I gave up my sons and wives.
I gave away my supreme, excellent head, legs, 
Arms, and eyes without ever being disheartened. {56}
{{milestone:{label:30.66,id:UT22084-055-001-2811}}}“Seeking this peace, this supreme samādhi,
I gave away wealth and grain, 
Hundreds of male and female slaves, and many jewels,
And satisfied numerous beggars. {57}
{{milestone:{label:30.67,id:UT22084-055-001-2812}}}“Seeking this peace, this supreme samādhi,
In the past I gave away great quantities 
Of pearls, crystals, gold, conches, ammonite stones,{{note:{index993,id:UT22084-055-001-2813}}} beryls,
Perfectly pure jewels, and a mass{{note:{index994,id:UT22084-055-001-2814}}} of coral, {58}
{{milestone:{label:30.68,id:UT22084-055-001-2815}}}“Seeking this peace, this supreme samādhi,
I gave away vast amounts of excellent jewelry 
Of various kinds, such as perfect strings of pearls, 
Lion jewelry,{{note:{index995,id:UT22084-055-001-2816}}} and nets of jewels. {59} {{page:{number:195,id:UT22084-055-001-6028,folio:F.98.b}}}
{{milestone:{label:30.69,id:UT22084-055-001-2817}}}“Seeking this peace, this supreme samādhi,
In the past I gave away many millions
Of fine, excellent clothes that were perfectly clean,
Made of the finest silk and cloth and beautified by gold threads. {60}
{{milestone:{label:30.70,id:UT22084-055-001-2818}}}“Seeking this peace, this supreme samādhi,
I gave away various kinds of elephants, horses, chariots, 
And my own beloved sons and women, 
Without ever experiencing any unhappiness. {61}
{{milestone:{label:30.71,id:UT22084-055-001-2819}}}“Seeking this peace, this supreme samādhi,
Whenever I saw people who were very poor,
Who were in distress and suffering because of their need,
I freed them from their poverty. {62}
{{milestone:{label:30.72,id:UT22084-055-001-2820}}}“Seeking this peace, this supreme samādhi,
I have in the past given to beggars
Trillions of{{note:{index996,id:UT22084-055-001-2821}}} horses, elephants, and chariots
Draped in nets of precious jewel adornments. {63}
{{milestone:{label:30.73,id:UT22084-055-001-2822}}}“Seeking this peace, this supreme samādhi,
I have in the past joyfully and with compassion
Given away many trillions 
Of excellently decorated parks. {64}
{{milestone:{label:30.74,id:UT22084-055-001-2823}}}“Seeking this peace, this supreme samādhi,
I have in the past given away beautifully adorned
Villages, towns, regions, and market towns,
And having given them felt continuous joy. {65}
{{milestone:{label:30.75,id:UT22084-055-001-2824}}}“Seeking this peace, this supreme samādhi,
I have in the past given to those who requested them
Heaps of jewels as large as Sumeru
And a similar amount of clothes and adornments. {66}
{{milestone:{label:30.76,id:UT22084-055-001-2825}}}“Seeking this peace, this supreme samādhi,
I have made those who are very poor rich,
I have protected those who were in great distress,
And I have made happy many who were enduring suffering. {67}
{{milestone:{label:30.77,id:UT22084-055-001-2826}}}“When I was a sovereign over this world
And saw the suffering of the population,
I felt compassion and wished them to be happy,
And gave my kingdom to them. {68}
{{milestone:{label:30.78,id:UT22084-055-001-2827}}}“Young man, the marvelous things that I have done,
And the hardships I have undergone for many hundreds of eons,
I would not be able to complete recounting them 
Even in a quintillion eons. {69}
{{milestone:{label:30.79,id:UT22084-055-001-2828}}}“Seeking this peace, this supreme samādhi,
I underwent astonishing hardships.
The people without faith in the Sugata’s conduct
Will have minds that become crazed and polluted. {70}
{{milestone:{label:30.80,id:UT22084-055-001-2829}}}“Young man, I declare this to you: {{page:{number:196,id:UT22084-055-001-6029,folio:F.99.a}}}
Have faith in me; my words are not untrue.
The Sugata does not speak words that are false.
The compassionate Jina always speaks the truth. {71}
{{milestone:{label:30.81,id:UT22084-055-001-2830}}}“These many different kinds of practices
I will have carried out for many{{note:{index997,id:UT22084-055-001-2831}}} eons.{{note:{index998,id:UT22084-055-001-2832}}}
However I attain this supreme samādhi 
I will then free millions of beings from suffering.{{note:{index999,id:UT22084-055-001-2833}}} {72}
{{milestone:{label:30.82,id:UT22084-055-001-2834}}}“In the moment that I have attained 
This samādhi, the path of great wisdom,
Having attained this supreme samādhi
I will see numerous millions of buddhas. {73}
{{milestone:{label:30.83,id:UT22084-055-001-2835}}}“I will have attained infinite miraculous powers,
And my emanations will go to hundreds of realms,
And there I will ask the compassionate ones
Many quintillions of questions. {74}
{{milestone:{label:30.84,id:UT22084-055-001-2836}}}“The sugatas will give me answers
For my quintillions of questions,
And having obtained them I will remember them all
And I will not forget even a single word. {75}
{{milestone:{label:30.85,id:UT22084-055-001-2837}}}“Having listened to the answers to those
Quintillions of correct questions,
I will teach the stainless state of peace
And establish many beings on the path of wisdom. {76}
{{milestone:{label:30.86,id:UT22084-055-001-2838}}}“I will remain in this samādhi
And train in it for many hundreds of eons,
And will first bring many quintillions of beings
On to the highest stainless path. {77}
{{milestone:{label:30.87,id:UT22084-055-001-2839}}}“Those who have not seen the previous sugatas
Who have taught this stainless way
Will not be able to have faith
In the supreme samādhi of emptiness, the ultimate truth. {78}
{{milestone:{label:30.88,id:UT22084-055-001-2840}}}“The people who have faith, are wise, and know the practice,
Are always joyful when they hear 
The way that is correct and profound,
And do not become frightened or terrified. {79}
{{milestone:{label:30.89,id:UT22084-055-001-2841}}}“They hold the supreme enlightenment.
They have been reborn as my sons.
They are like fig-tree flowers,
And I practice for hundreds of eons for their sake. {80}
{{milestone:{label:30.90,id:UT22084-055-001-2842}}}“They who possess this supreme samādhi
Have no fear of falling into unfortunate existences,
Are always free of the eight disadvantageous states,
And will see numerous millions of buddhas. {81}
{{milestone:{label:30.91,id:UT22084-055-001-2843}}}“They who have this supreme samādhi in their hands, {{page:{number:197,id:UT22084-055-001-6030,folio:F.99.b}}}
I prophesy, will have unending understanding,
And like the kind Jina{{note:{index1000,id:UT22084-055-001-2844}}} who has infinite fame,{{note:{index1001,id:UT22084-055-001-2845}}}
They will accomplish many benefits for beings. {82}
{{milestone:{label:30.92,id:UT22084-055-001-2846}}}“They who possess this samādhi
Will have understanding and memory,
High wisdom, will retain what they have heard,
And will possess vast confidence of speech. {83}
{{milestone:{label:30.93,id:UT22084-055-001-2847}}}“They who possess this samādhi
Will receive the offerings of devas,
Will be continually revered by humans,{{note:{index1002,id:UT22084-055-001-2848}}}
And will be constantly protected by the hosts of spirits.{{note:{index1003,id:UT22084-055-001-2849}}} {84}
{{milestone:{label:30.94,id:UT22084-055-001-2850}}}“They who possess this supreme samādhi
Do not die in fire or water,
Are not harmed by poison or weapons,
And cannot be reached by enemies. {85}
{{milestone:{label:30.95,id:UT22084-055-001-2851}}}“They who possess this supreme samādhi
Will always dwell in forest bowers,
Where they will be constantly attended by devas, 
And where many yakṣas will be their servants. {86}
{{milestone:{label:30.96,id:UT22084-055-001-2852}}}“They who possess this supreme samādhi
Will have wisdom that is as vast as the ocean,
Will describe without impediment the qualities of the Sage,
And make known correctly the qualities of the Buddha. {87}
{{milestone:{label:30.97,id:UT22084-055-001-2853}}}“They who possess this supreme samādhi
Will have endless, boundless learning
That is beyond measure, like space,
And will hold the torch of wisdom that dispels darkness. {88}
{{milestone:{label:30.98,id:UT22084-055-001-2854}}}“They who possess this supreme samādhi 
Will always be gentle, will speak appropriate words,
Will be beloved in the midst of their followers,
And their speech will be like the lion’s roar. {89}
{{milestone:{label:30.99,id:UT22084-055-001-2855}}}“They who possess this supreme samādhi
Will be like healing physicians,
The support, protector, and refuge of many,
And will bring illumination to the worlds. {90}
{{milestone:{label:30.100,id:UT22084-055-001-2856}}}“They who possess this supreme samādhi
Will not take pleasure in sexual intercourse.{{note:{index1004,id:UT22084-055-001-2857}}}
They will enjoy śamatha and reach the bliss of dhyāna.
With a peaceful voice{{note:{index1005,id:UT22084-055-001-2858}}} they will speak of peace. {91}
{{milestone:{label:30.101,id:UT22084-055-001-2859}}}“They who possess this supreme samādhi
Will not take pleasure in conceptualization,
Will be free of the entire multitude of concepts,
And those wise ones will constantly be in meditation. {{page:{number:198,id:UT22084-055-001-6031,folio:F.100.a}}} {92}
{{milestone:{label:30.102,id:UT22084-055-001-2860}}}“They who possess this supreme samādhi
Will attain extraordinary vision
And will see the infinite jinas.
They will be leaders with infinite sight. {93}
{{milestone:{label:30.103,id:UT22084-055-001-2861}}}“They who possess this supreme samādhi
Will have the sweet and melodious voice of a crane,{{note:{index1006,id:UT22084-055-001-2862}}}
The sound of the avadavat and a drumbeat,{{note:{index1007,id:UT22084-055-001-2863}}}
And a singing sound and gentle voice. {94}
{{milestone:{label:30.104,id:UT22084-055-001-2864}}}“They who possess this supreme samādhi
Will have a voice that is like resounding thunder.
Their gentle speech will be like the song of a goose
And their voice will have the fifty aspects of speech.{{note:{index1008,id:UT22084-055-001-2865}}} {95}
{{milestone:{label:30.105,id:UT22084-055-001-2866}}}“They who possess this supreme samādhi
Will speak with an inconceivable voice
That has the pleasant sound of the various aspects of speech 
For numerous quintillions of eons. {96}
{{milestone:{label:30.106,id:UT22084-055-001-2867}}}“They who possess this supreme samādhi
Will not have attachment to food,
Will not delight in alms bowls or dharma robes,
But with few desires they will be content and abstinent. {97}
{{milestone:{label:30.107,id:UT22084-055-001-2868}}}“They who possess this supreme samādhi
Do not praise themselves
And never criticize others.
They always delight in dhyāna and have a subtle mind. {98}
{{milestone:{label:30.108,id:UT22084-055-001-2869}}}“They who possess this supreme samādhi
Always examine themselves,
Do not look for mistakes in others,
And the entire world does not impede them. {99}
{{milestone:{label:30.109,id:UT22084-055-001-2870}}}“They who possess this supreme samādhi
Have pure conduct and untroubled minds,
Are never deceitful or dishonest,
Are always gentle, and always delight in liberation. {100}
{{milestone:{label:30.110,id:UT22084-055-001-2871}}}“They who possess this supreme samādhi
Are always motivated to generosity,
Take no delight in avarice,
And always have correct conduct. {101}
{{milestone:{label:30.111,id:UT22084-055-001-2872}}}“They who possess this supreme samādhi
Are handsome, good looking, and attractive.
Their bodies shine like the purest gold
And have the thirty-two primary signs of a great being. {102}
{{milestone:{label:30.112,id:UT22084-055-001-2873}}}“They who possess this supreme samādhi
Always have an attractive appearance,
Are observed and beloved by many people, {{page:{number:199,id:UT22084-055-001-6032,folio:F.100.b}}}
And those people never have enough of gazing upon them. {103}
{{milestone:{label:30.113,id:UT22084-055-001-2874}}}“They who possess this supreme samādhi
Always delight, gladden, and enchant
Devas, nāgas, and likewise the yakṣas,
Who enter towns{{note:{index1009,id:UT22084-055-001-2875}}} and praise them.{{note:{index1010,id:UT22084-055-001-2876}}} {104}
{{milestone:{label:30.114,id:UT22084-055-001-2877}}}“They who possess this supreme samādhi
Always have Brahmā, Śakra, and many powerful deities
Acting as their attendants,
But there is no pride in their minds. {105}
{{milestone:{label:30.115,id:UT22084-055-001-2878}}}“They who possess this supreme samādhi
Have no fear of the lower existences.
They have no fear of the disadvantageous existences or bad rebirths.
They are completely free of all fear of bad rebirths. {106}
{{milestone:{label:30.116,id:UT22084-055-001-2879}}}“They who possess this supreme samādhi
Have no doubts or uncertainties 
On hearing in detail the supreme Dharma of the Buddha,
And they follow that profound wisdom. {107}
{{milestone:{label:30.117,id:UT22084-055-001-2880}}}“They who possess this supreme samādhi,
Whatever subtle Dharma teachings they hear
They attain perfect mastery of them all,
And gain their power and detailed reasoning. {108}
{{milestone:{label:30.118,id:UT22084-055-001-2881}}}“They who possess this supreme samādhi
Constantly think, ‘I will always act in accordance
With what the Jina’s words have taught,’
And attain unique, supreme retention. {109}
{{milestone:{label:30.119,id:UT22084-055-001-2882}}}“They who possess this supreme samādhi
Will, when the time of their death comes,
Have before them the compassionate Amitābha
And his host of bhikṣus.{{note:{index1011,id:UT22084-055-001-2883}}} {110}
{{milestone:{label:30.120,id:UT22084-055-001-2884}}}“They who possess this supreme samādhi
Are those who have attained the retentions,
Have perfect mastery over the treasure of the Dharma,
And possess the unceasing words of eloquence. {111}
{{milestone:{label:30.121,id:UT22084-055-001-2885}}}“They who possess this supreme samādhi,
With peaceful conduct and peaceful{{note:{index1012,id:UT22084-055-001-2886}}} minds
Will be an illumination for beings
Wherever those holders of the Dharma go.{{note:{index1013,id:UT22084-055-001-2887}}} {112}
{{milestone:{label:30.122,id:UT22084-055-001-2888}}}“They attain the ten bhūmis:{{note:{index1014,id:UT22084-055-001-2889}}}Perfect Joy, 
Stainless, Shining, Brilliance, Difficult to Master, 
Manifest, Gone Far, Unwavering, 
Perfect Understanding, and Clouds of Dharma.{{note:{index1015,id:UT22084-055-001-2890}}} {i}
{{milestone:{label:30.123,id:UT22084-055-001-2891}}}“Those heroes attain the ten powers:{{note:{index1016,id:UT22084-055-001-2892}}}
Life,{{note:{index1017,id:UT22084-055-001-2893}}} karma,{{note:{index1018,id:UT22084-055-001-2894}}} materials,{{note:{index1019,id:UT22084-055-001-2895}}} and devotion,{{note:{index1020,id:UT22084-055-001-2896}}}
And the strengths of aspiration,{{note:{index1021,id:UT22084-055-001-2897}}} miracles,{{note:{index1022,id:UT22084-055-001-2898}}} and birth,{{note:{index1023,id:UT22084-055-001-2899}}}{{page:{number:200,id:UT22084-055-001-6033,folio:F.101.a}}}
Dharma,{{note:{index1024,id:UT22084-055-001-2900}}} mind,{{note:{index1025,id:UT22084-055-001-2901}}} and likewise great wisdom.{{note:{index1026,id:UT22084-055-001-2902}}} {ii}
{{milestone:{label:30.124,id:UT22084-055-001-2903}}}“They who possess this supreme samādhi
Are skilled in the various aspects of the supreme Dharma treasure,
Have attained the perfect power of the dharmakāya,
And cut through the doubts of all beings.{{note:{index1027,id:UT22084-055-001-2904}}} {113}
{{milestone:{label:30.125,id:UT22084-055-001-2905}}}“If all beings were compassionate bhagavāns,
And were sugatas until existence comes to an end,
And if someone were to make offerings to them for many hundreds of eons 
Or for more eons than there are sand grains in the Ganges, {114}
{{milestone:{label:30.126,id:UT22084-055-001-2906}}}“And if in this latter time of destruction
Someone were to hear this samādhi
And say only the words ‘I rejoice in this!’
The previous merit would not be a fraction of this accumulation. {115}
{{milestone:{label:30.127,id:UT22084-055-001-2907}}}“Young man, whoever has this practice of peace,
This supreme samādhi, the ultimate truth of emptiness,
Propagates it and creates copies of it,
That one is a dharmabhāṇaka with wisdom.” {116}
{{milestone:{label:30.128,id:UT22084-055-001-2908}}}Conclusion of the thirtieth chapter, “Tejaguṇarāja.”
{{milestone:{label:31,id:UT22084-055-001-chapter-31}}}Benefits
Chapter 31
{{milestone:{label:31.1,id:UT22084-055-001-2909}}}Then the Bhagavān said to the youth Candraprabha, “Therefore, young man, bodhisattva mahāsattvas who think, ‘I shall understand the languages of all beings and, knowing their higher or lesser capabilities, I will teach them the Dharma,’ those bodhisattva mahāsattvas should listen to the samādhi, the revealed equality of the nature of all phenomena, learn it, understand it, keep it, recite it to others, promote it, proclaim it, chant it, meditate on it with unadulterated meditation, promulgate it, and make it widely known to others.”
Thereupon the Bhagavān spoke these verses:
{{milestone:{label:31.2,id:UT22084-055-001-2911}}}“They who, desiring liberation, possess this stainless samādhi
See the countless guides of the past,
Ask those lords of the world about their previous practice, 
And those bodhisattvas dwell in supreme roots of merit. {1}
{{milestone:{label:31.3,id:UT22084-055-001-2912}}}“They who, desiring liberation, possess this stainless samādhi
Obtain the highest happiness of devas and humans, {{page:{number:201,id:UT22084-055-001-6034,folio:F.101.b}}}
Obtain the supreme offerings of devas and humans,
And obtain the happiness of dhyāna, the supreme, noble happiness.{{note:{index1028,id:UT22084-055-001-2913}}} {2}
{{milestone:{label:31.4,id:UT22084-055-001-2914}}}“They who, desiring liberation, possess this stainless samādhi
Do not become thrilled on hearing the highest praises,
Do not become saddened by being criticized,
And like a mountain are unmoved by the eight worldly concerns. {3}
{{milestone:{label:31.5,id:UT22084-055-001-2915}}}“They who, desiring liberation, possess this stainless samādhi
Speak perfectly{{note:{index1029,id:UT22084-055-001-2916}}} pleasantly, with gentle words,
Do not frown, always speak sincerely,
Have a smiling face, and have been instructed by the guides. {4}
{{milestone:{label:31.6,id:UT22084-055-001-2917}}}“They who, desiring liberation, possess this stainless samādhi
Are pleasant, good company, have a gentle mind,
Are always restrained{{note:{index1030,id:UT22084-055-001-2918}}} and established in self-discipline,
And are very gentle, have pleasing speech,{{note:{index1031,id:UT22084-055-001-2919}}} and speak tenderly.{{note:{index1032,id:UT22084-055-001-2920}}} {5}
{{milestone:{label:31.7,id:UT22084-055-001-2921}}}“They who, desiring liberation, possess this stainless samādhi
Do not quarrel or cause conflict when they speak.
They have freed themselves from all stubbornness{{note:{index1033,id:UT22084-055-001-2922}}} and anger 
And are always joyful,{{note:{index1034,id:UT22084-055-001-2923}}} pleasant, and gentle. {6}
{{milestone:{label:31.8,id:UT22084-055-001-2924}}}“They who, desiring liberation, possess this stainless samādhi
Are always wise and are constantly motivated to generosity.
When they see beings in great suffering they give them their food;
They delight in giving to others, and not in their own enjoyment. {7}
{{milestone:{label:31.9,id:UT22084-055-001-2925}}}“They who, desiring liberation, possess this stainless samādhi
Are admired by a hundred thousand devas, 
Are always attended by nāgas, asuras, and yakṣas,
And are protected by those who dwell in the forest and its environs.{{note:{index1035,id:UT22084-055-001-2926}}} {8}
{{milestone:{label:31.10,id:UT22084-055-001-2927}}}“They speak with unimpeded words, like the voice of Brahmā,
Have a voice like the song of a goose, a voice like a kinnara’s song,{{note:{index1036,id:UT22084-055-001-2928}}}
Have the fifty aspects of speech and have a sound that brings joy,{{note:{index1037,id:UT22084-055-001-2929}}}
And have a resounding voice, a proclaiming voice, a perfect voice.{{note:{index1038,id:UT22084-055-001-2930}}} {9}
{{milestone:{label:31.11,id:UT22084-055-001-2931}}}“Even if someone knew how to reduce
All the worlds into their smallest particles,
They who possess this supreme, stainless samādhi
Would voice sounds that were even more numerous. {10}
{{milestone:{label:31.12,id:UT22084-055-001-2932}}}“They who possess this stainless samādhi
Attain the ten powers, and attain the eight and two bhūmis.
The wise ones attain the inconceivable qualities of a buddha, {{page:{number:202,id:UT22084-055-001-6035,folio:F.102.a}}}
Subjugate all māras, and reach the highest enlightenment.”{{note:{index1039,id:UT22084-055-001-2933}}} {i}
{{milestone:{label:31.13,id:UT22084-055-001-2934}}}Conclusion of the thirty-first chapter, “Benefits.”
{{milestone:{label:32,id:UT22084-055-001-chapter-32}}}The Teaching on the Nature of All Phenomena
Chapter 32
{{milestone:{label:32.1,id:UT22084-055-001-2935}}}Then the Bhagavān said to the youth Candraprabha, “Therefore, young man, bodhisattva mahāsattvas who wonder, ‘How can I know the nature of all phenomena?’ should listen to this samādhi, the revealed equality of the nature of all phenomena, learn it, understand it, keep it, recite it to others, promote it, proclaim it, chant it, meditate on it with unadulterated meditation, promulgate it, and make it widely known to others.”
Thereupon the Bhagavān spoke these verses:
{{milestone:{label:32.2,id:UT22084-055-001-2937}}}“In the ones who know the peace that is the nature of phenomena 
No desire arises, no anger arises, 
Nor in those great leaders does ignorance ever arise.
They have eliminated all kleśas without remainder. {1}
{{milestone:{label:32.3,id:UT22084-055-001-2938}}}“They who know the peace that is the nature of phenomena 
Are heart children of the Sugata who do not abandon the training.
They are heroes who never fall under the power of women.
Everywhere they rejoice in the teaching of the sugatas. {2}
{{milestone:{label:32.4,id:UT22084-055-001-2939}}}“They who know the peace that is the nature of phenomena 
Are wise, sagacious, and know the way of wisdom.{{note:{index1040,id:UT22084-055-001-2940}}}
They see infinite, endless buddhas
And know infinite dhāraṇīs{{note:{index1041,id:UT22084-055-001-2941}}} and wisdom.{{note:{index1042,id:UT22084-055-001-2942}}} {3}
{{milestone:{label:32.5,id:UT22084-055-001-2943}}}“They who know the peace that is the nature of phenomena
Will before long become a lord of humans.
They know the skills of healing and bestow happiness,{{note:{index1043,id:UT22084-055-001-2944}}}
And they are able to remove all the pain of suffering.{{note:{index1044,id:UT22084-055-001-2945}}} {4}
{{milestone:{label:32.6,id:UT22084-055-001-2946}}}“They who know the peace that is the nature of phenomena 
Know that sentient beings are suffering.
They always beat the drum of the elixir.
They will before long become a guide.{{note:{index1045,id:UT22084-055-001-2947}}} {5}
{{milestone:{label:32.7,id:UT22084-055-001-2948}}}“They are the supreme physicians, skilled in healing.
They know the origin of all illnesses and how to be freed from them. {{page:{number:203,id:UT22084-055-001-6036,folio:F.102.b}}}
They have wisdom and train correctly.
Having trained they liberate many lost beings. {6}
{{milestone:{label:32.8,id:UT22084-055-001-2949}}}“They who know the peace that is the nature of phenomena 
Are wise heroes who are skilled in the nature of emptiness.
They have no attachment to the world and always their food is alms,
And they bring many beings to supreme enlightenment.{{note:{index1046,id:UT22084-055-001-2950}}} {7}
{{milestone:{label:32.9,id:UT22084-055-001-2951}}}“They who know the peace that is the nature of phenomena{{note:{index1047,id:UT22084-055-001-2952}}}
Are moons{{note:{index1048,id:UT22084-055-001-2953}}} among people, superior through the power of patience.
They are not angry even if struck with stones and sticks,
And they are not disturbed even if their limbs are severed. {8}
{{milestone:{label:32.10,id:UT22084-055-001-2954}}}“They who know the peace that is the nature of phenomena 
Have the strength of being established in the strength of patience.{{note:{index1049,id:UT22084-055-001-2955}}}
Not seeing a thing that is tolerated, they are perfectly at peace.{{note:{index1050,id:UT22084-055-001-2956}}}
They are wise heroes who do not become proud of the strength of their patience.{{note:{index1051,id:UT22084-055-001-2957}}} {9}
{{milestone:{label:32.11,id:UT22084-055-001-2958}}}“They who know the peace that is the nature of phenomena, 
Never have in mind the idea ‘I am cutting through things’;
For them all things are nonexistent, always empty,
And they have eliminated every single conceptual identification. {10}
{{milestone:{label:32.12,id:UT22084-055-001-2959}}}“Such are they who teach the supreme nature of phenomena.
They will before long reach the highest enlightenment.
They comprehend the scope of the nature of phenomena.
They give a gift that is infinite and endless. {11}
{{milestone:{label:32.13,id:UT22084-055-001-2960}}}“They who know the peace that is the nature of phenomena 
Teach infinite millions of sūtras
That are more numerous than sand grains in the Ganges,
And there is no interruption in their eloquence. {12}
{{milestone:{label:32.14,id:UT22084-055-001-2961}}}“They who know the peace that is the nature of phenomena 
Have wisdom as high as Sumeru,
Constantly for a hundred trillion eons,
And their teaching of the Dharma knows no end. {13}
{{milestone:{label:32.15,id:UT22084-055-001-2962}}}“They who know the peace that is the nature of phenomena 
Have a vast, abundant, inconceivable eloquence.
They constantly seek supreme enlightenment
And teach infinite millions of sūtras. {14}
{{milestone:{label:32.16,id:UT22084-055-001-2963}}}“They who know that these phenomena have no substance
Perfectly hear and remember the entirety 
Of the Dharma that the lords of humans have taught {{page:{number:204,id:UT22084-055-001-6037,folio:F.103.a}}}
And do not doubt even a single word. {15}
{{milestone:{label:32.17,id:UT22084-055-001-2964}}}“They who know that phenomena are always empty
Are at all times uniquely superior in their generosity.
They are patrons who give happiness to those who suffer.
When they see beings suffer they satisfy them with jewels. {16}
{{milestone:{label:32.18,id:UT22084-055-001-2965}}}“They who know that phenomena are always empty 
Will always become the kings of Jambudhvaja.
At all times they have love for all the living
And always bring infinite happiness to beings. {17}
{{milestone:{label:32.19,id:UT22084-055-001-2966}}}“They who know that phenomena are always empty
Are heroes who give away their sons, daughters, and slaves.
Those great leaders’ minds never waver,
As they give away their hands, their feet, their head, and their kingdom. {18}
{{milestone:{label:32.20,id:UT22084-055-001-2967}}}“They who know that phenomena are always empty
Have no anger in their mind, even in a dream,
Even though their limbs are cut from their body;
For them it is an offering to the guides, the lords of humans. {19}
{{milestone:{label:32.21,id:UT22084-055-001-2968}}}“They who know that phenomena are always empty
Make offerings to all the guides of the past,
Make offerings to the lords of humans in the future,
And venerate all the guides in the present. {20}
{{milestone:{label:32.22,id:UT22084-055-001-2969}}}“They who hear and retain this sūtra in the degenerate times
Are wise individuals who possess the treasure of the sugatas.
They are established in the supreme retentions,{{note:{index1052,id:UT22084-055-001-2970}}}
And before long will become guides of the worlds. {21}
{{milestone:{label:32.23,id:UT22084-055-001-2971}}}“They who do not forget but teach this sūtra
Are wise individuals who will never become blind.
Throughout many eons they will not lose a limb,
And will always avoid the eight disadvantageous states. {22}
{{milestone:{label:32.24,id:UT22084-055-001-2972}}}“They will never be reborn in the lower existences.
They will always have a beautiful body with the primary signs of a great being.
They will always cultivate the five higher cognitions,
And those heroes will always be in the presence of the sugatas. {23}
{{milestone:{label:32.25,id:UT22084-055-001-2973}}}“Endowed with wisdom they will manifest many emanations
That will go to millions of realms to guide beings. 
Of all those who see this multitude of buddha emanations, {{page:{number:205,id:UT22084-055-001-6038,folio:F.103.b}}}
That many beings will be brought to supreme enlightenment. {24}
{{milestone:{label:32.26,id:UT22084-055-001-2974}}}They who hear and retain this sūtra in the degenerate times
Will be endowed with memory, understanding, wisdom, and constancy.
They will become powerful through the strength of their diligence.
They will have great brilliance and they will reach the culmination of the Dharma. {25}
{{milestone:{label:32.27,id:UT22084-055-001-2975}}}They who hold this samādhi of peace in the degenerate time
Are heroes established in the brahmavihāras.
They quickly attain the eight and two bhūmis,
And swiftly subjugate the māras.{{note:{index1053,id:UT22084-055-001-2976}}} {i}
{{milestone:{label:32.28,id:UT22084-055-001-2977}}}Those who always meditate on this sūtra of peace
Will attain power and possess the highest strengths.
They will always be ones who are intent on benefiting beings,
And will realize the highest enlightenment at the foot of the Bodhi tree.{{note:{index1054,id:UT22084-055-001-2978}}} {ii}
{{milestone:{label:32.29,id:UT22084-055-001-2979}}}“Those who meditate that these phenomena are empty
Constantly radiate ten billion light rays
And eclipse even the disks of the suns.
Those heroes will, before long, become guides of the worlds. {26}
{{milestone:{label:32.30,id:UT22084-055-001-2980}}}“In the past I practiced this field of peace
For many quintillions of eons.
My diligence upon this path was unceasing
And Dīpaṃkara prophesied I would become a jina. {27}
{{milestone:{label:32.31,id:UT22084-055-001-2981}}}“You also should follow my practice of this sūtra,
This teaching that leads to the profound ultimate truth.
There are many tīrthikas who are lost in error concerning this. 
They revile enlightenment and fall into the terrible lower realms. {28}
{{milestone:{label:32.32,id:UT22084-055-001-2982}}}“During many quintillions of eons
They will experience unendurable sufferings of heat.
And even after many millions of eons have passed
They will still not die for that reason. {29}
{{milestone:{label:32.33,id:UT22084-055-001-2983}}}“Those who in the terrible latter times
Protect this sūtra of the Sugata, this state of peace, 
Will attain the highest enlightenment without difficulty. 
They are the prophesied holders of the Dharma in the future.” {30}
{{milestone:{label:32.34,id:UT22084-055-001-2984}}}Conclusion of the thirty-second chapter, “The Teaching on the Nature of All Phenomena.”{{note:{index1055,id:UT22084-055-001-2985}}}{{page:{number:206,id:UT22084-055-001-6039,folio:F.104.a}}}
{{milestone:{label:33,id:UT22084-055-001-chapter-33}}}The Benefits of Possessing the Sūtra
Chapter 33
{{milestone:{label:33.1,id:UT22084-055-001-2986}}} Then the Bhagavān said to the youth Candraprabha, “Therefore, young man, bodhisattva mahāsattvas who wish to train in purifying{{note:{index1056,id:UT22084-055-001-2987}}} the great higher cognition of all phenomena should listen to the samādhi, the revealed equality of the nature of all phenomena, learn it, understand it, keep it, recite it to others, promote it, proclaim it, chant it, meditate on it with unadulterated meditation, promulgate it, and make it widely known to others.{{note:{index1057,id:UT22084-055-001-2988}}}
{{milestone:{label:33.2,id:UT22084-055-001-2989}}}“Young man, what is the purification of the great higher cognition of all phenomena? It is having no grasping toward all phenomena, it is having no clinging to the aggregate of correct conduct,{{note:{index1058,id:UT22084-055-001-2990}}} it is having no pride in the aggregate of samādhi, it is the absence of movement in the aggregate of wisdom, it is having the discerning insight{{note:{index1059,id:UT22084-055-001-2991}}} of the aggregate of liberation, and it is seeing correctly as it is the aggregate of the insight of the wisdom of liberation.{{note:{index1060,id:UT22084-055-001-2992}}}
{{milestone:{label:33.3,id:UT22084-055-001-2993}}}“The bodhisattva mahāsattva who has those higher cognitions manifests all the manifestations of samādhi and teaches the Dharma to beings. 
“This, young man, is what is called ‘the purification of the great higher cognition of all phenomena.’ ” 
{{milestone:{label:33.4,id:UT22084-055-001-2995}}}Then at that time the Bhagavān gave a detailed Dharma teaching on purifying the great higher cognition of all phenomena by chanting the following extensive verses to the youth Candraprabha:
{{milestone:{label:33.5,id:UT22084-055-001-2996}}}“The purification of the great higher cognitions
Is an incontrovertible teaching.
Someone who practices in contradiction to it
Will not become free of attachment. {1}
{{milestone:{label:33.6,id:UT22084-055-001-2997}}}“That higher cognition, that wisdom,
Is the inconceivable wisdom of buddhahood.
Someone who remains in attachment
Will never know that wisdom. {2}
{{milestone:{label:33.7,id:UT22084-055-001-2998}}}“The numerous inconceivable Dharmas
Are taught by using words.
Someone who is attached to words
Will not know the meaning of the teaching. {3} {{page:{number:207,id:UT22084-055-001-6040,folio:F.104.b}}}
{{milestone:{label:33.8,id:UT22084-055-001-2999}}}“How can someone teach the meaning
Who does not know the meaning behind the words?
Someone who has not learned what the true nature is
Teaches that which is not the Dharma as the Dharma. {4}
{{milestone:{label:33.9,id:UT22084-055-001-3000}}}“The one meaning of the differing words
Of the sūtras that have been taught by me
Within thousands of worlds
Is something that cannot be stated. {5}
{{milestone:{label:33.10,id:UT22084-055-001-3001}}}“Through contemplating a single word
All of them will be meditated on—
All of the many kinds of Dharma that have been taught
By however many buddhas there have been. {6}
{{milestone:{label:33.11,id:UT22084-055-001-3002}}}“For people who have mastered the meaning
That all phenomena are selfless,{{note:{index1061,id:UT22084-055-001-3003}}}
When they have learned this word
The Dharmas of the Buddha will not be hard to attain.{{note:{index1062,id:UT22084-055-001-3004}}} {7}
{{milestone:{label:33.12,id:UT22084-055-001-3005}}}“All phenomena are the Buddha’s Dharma.{{note:{index1063,id:UT22084-055-001-3006}}}
They who have learned the nature of phenomena,
They know the nature of phenomena 
And do not contradict the nature of phenomena. {8}
{{milestone:{label:33.13,id:UT22084-055-001-3007}}}“All words are the Buddha’s words,
As all words have no substance.
Although one seeks them in the ten directions
The words of the Buddha will not be found. {9}
{{milestone:{label:33.14,id:UT22084-055-001-3008}}}“These words are the Buddha’s words.
Though one seeks them in the ten directions, 
These unsurpassable words are not to be found.
They have never been found and never will be found.{{note:{index1064,id:UT22084-055-001-3009}}} {10}
{{milestone:{label:33.15,id:UT22084-055-001-3010}}}“The Buddha’s words are unsurpassable.
There is nothing higher than the Buddha’s words.
There is not an atom of them that is to be found,
And that is why they are called unsurpassable. {11}
{{milestone:{label:33.16,id:UT22084-055-001-3011}}}“An atom, a phenomenon, is not produced.
Although explanations use the term ‘atom,’
Something the size of an atom cannot be found;
It is a term used in teaching on the worldly level. {12}
{{milestone:{label:33.17,id:UT22084-055-001-3012}}}“The unfindability of phenomena is found,
But that finding also cannot be found. 
Thus they who know phenomena 
Realize the highest enlightenment, {13}
{{milestone:{label:33.18,id:UT22084-055-001-3013}}}“And having realized the highest enlightenment
They will turn the wheel of the Dharma.
Through turning the wheel of the Dharma
They teach the Buddha’s Dharma. {14}
{{milestone:{label:33.19,id:UT22084-055-001-3014}}}“The bodhisattvas who realize
The highest wisdom of buddhahood,
Because of that are called buddhas,
As they have realized buddhahood’s wisdom. {15}
{{milestone:{label:33.20,id:UT22084-055-001-3015}}}“The absence of existents, the absence of aspiration,
The absence of attributes, and emptiness—
It is these doorways to liberation
That the Buddha taught as doorways. {16}
{{milestone:{label:33.21,id:UT22084-055-001-3016}}}“The eyes, the ears, and the nose,
The tongue, the body, and likewise the mind,
The buddhas have explained 
That they are by nature empty. {17}
{{milestone:{label:33.22,id:UT22084-055-001-3017}}}“They who know in that way
The nature of phenomena, {{page:{number:208,id:UT22084-055-001-6041,folio:F.105.a}}}
Knowing the characteristics of phenomena, 
They will not be in disagreement with it. {18}
{{milestone:{label:33.23,id:UT22084-055-001-3018}}}“This is the realm of experience of the heroes,
Of the bodhisattvas, the protectors.
They know the emptiness of phenomena
And they never have any doubt. {19}
{{milestone:{label:33.24,id:UT22084-055-001-3019}}}“Those who know the nature of phenomena,
Those ones are called a buddha.
They guide countless, innumerable 
Beings to enlightenment. {20}
{{milestone:{label:33.25,id:UT22084-055-001-3020}}}“That which is accomplished by the word buddha
Is also accomplished by the words correct conduct.
The words buddha and correct conduct
Have the same characteristic. {21}
{{milestone:{label:33.26,id:UT22084-055-001-3021}}}“However many{{note:{index1065,id:UT22084-055-001-3022}}} words are spoken 
Whether superior, middling, or lesser,
They are all taught in the one word meditation,
And in the one word buddha. {22}
{{milestone:{label:33.27,id:UT22084-055-001-3023}}}“The Buddha’s Dharma{{note:{index1066,id:UT22084-055-001-3024}}} is stated
To have no location and no direction.
It has no birth and no cessation.
Neither is it single nor multiple. {23}
{{milestone:{label:33.28,id:UT22084-055-001-3025}}}“It is not new and it is not old.
There is nothing to be proud of.
It is not blue and it is not yellow;
Neither is it white, nor red. {24}
{{milestone:{label:33.29,id:UT22084-055-001-3026}}}“That which is taught through verses
Is inexpressible and ungraspable.
This miraculous activity of the Sage
Is beyond the level of verses. {25}
{{milestone:{label:33.30,id:UT22084-055-001-3027}}}{26}{{note:{index1067,id:UT22084-055-001-3028}}}
{{milestone:{label:33.31,id:UT22084-055-001-3029}}}“The buddha who has passed into nirvāṇa
Is seen in the form of a buddha.
The one who imagines that he is present
Will also see the buddha’s miracles. {27}
{{milestone:{label:33.32,id:UT22084-055-001-3030}}}“When someone has reached nirvāṇa
There is no being that is to be found.
That is how the Dharma is taught
And many beings are liberated. {28}
{{milestone:{label:33.33,id:UT22084-055-001-3031}}}“Just as the sun and moon
Appear in a bronze bowl
Without their own form going there,
Such is the nature of phenomena. {29}
{{milestone:{label:33.34,id:UT22084-055-001-3032}}}“Those who know the nature
Of phenomena to be like reflections,{{note:{index1068,id:UT22084-055-001-3033}}}
They do not see the Buddha’s body
As being a body of form.{{note:{index1069,id:UT22084-055-001-3034}}} {30}
{{milestone:{label:33.35,id:UT22084-055-001-3035}}}“This phenomenon has no body;{{note:{index1070,id:UT22084-055-001-3036}}}
There is no body in it at all.
A phenomenon has no body,
And that is the body of the Buddha. {31}
{{milestone:{label:33.36,id:UT22084-055-001-3037}}}“Those who see the dharmakāya, {{page:{number:209,id:UT22084-055-001-6042,folio:F.105.b}}}
They are the ones who see the Guide.
The dharmakāyas{{note:{index1071,id:UT22084-055-001-3038}}} are the buddhas.
That is seeing the buddhas. {32}
{{milestone:{label:33.37,id:UT22084-055-001-3039}}}“That which is specified through dependence
Is specified to not be specific. 
Those who wish to be renunciants
Should understand this approach. {33}
{{milestone:{label:33.38,id:UT22084-055-001-3040}}}{34}{{note:{index1072,id:UT22084-055-001-3041}}}
{{milestone:{label:33.39,id:UT22084-055-001-3042}}}“Whoever thinks, ‘I have attained,’
Is for that reason said to be without attainment. 
The one who is said to be a renunciant
Is the one who thinks, ‘I have not attained renuncation.’ {35}
{{milestone:{label:33.40,id:UT22084-055-001-3043}}}“Those who have not learned this profundity, 
How can they teach the Dharma? 
They cannot describe it
Through using profound words. {36}
{{milestone:{label:33.41,id:UT22084-055-001-3044}}}“The five skandhas are insubstantial.
Being nonexistent they arise.
For the one to whom the skandhas arise,
There is nothing that arises. {37}
{{milestone:{label:33.42,id:UT22084-055-001-3045}}}“Those characteristics of the skandhas
Are the characteristics of all phenomena.
Those characteristics are taught 
But there are no characteristics that exist. {38}
{{milestone:{label:33.43,id:UT22084-055-001-3046}}}“The characteristic of phenomena
Is the same as that of space and sky,
As seen in the past, the future,
And as in the present. {39}
{{milestone:{label:33.44,id:UT22084-055-001-3047}}}“Space is taught to be ungraspable;
There is nothing there to be grasped.
That is the nature of phenomena:
It is ungraspable like space. {40}
{{milestone:{label:33.45,id:UT22084-055-001-3048}}}“That is how phenomena are taught,
That there is nothing to be seen.
For the one who does not see phenomena,
Phenomena are beyond conception. {41}
{{milestone:{label:33.46,id:UT22084-055-001-3049}}}“These phenomena have no nature;
They have no nature to be found.
For those dedicated to buddhahood’s enlightenment
This is the domain of the yogin. {42}
{{milestone:{label:33.47,id:UT22084-055-001-3050}}}“The ones who know phenomena in that way
Will not have attachment to phenomena.
Not being attached to phenomena,
They understand the conceptualization of phenomena. {43}
{{milestone:{label:33.48,id:UT22084-055-001-3051}}}“The bodhisattvas, the protectors,
Have annihilated all phenomena.
Having annihilated the conceptualization of phenomena
They do not become proud in the Buddha’s Dharma. {44}
{{milestone:{label:33.49,id:UT22084-055-001-3052}}}“Having no pride in that preeminence,
They examine and teach that preeminence.
The ones who know that preeminence
Will have no pride throughout ten million eons. {45}
{{milestone:{label:33.50,id:UT22084-055-001-3053}}}“The foolish examine that preeminence
And subsequently continue in saṃsāra.
It has no location that can be found
Even though one searches throughout the ten directions. {46}
{{milestone:{label:33.51,id:UT22084-055-001-3054}}}“The bodhisattva,{{note:{index1073,id:UT22084-055-001-3055}}} knowing emptiness, 
Has no attachment to saṃsāra.{{note:{index1074,id:UT22084-055-001-3056}}}{{page:{number:210,id:UT22084-055-001-6043,folio:F.106.a}}}
They{{note:{index1075,id:UT22084-055-001-3057}}} practice to attain enlightenment
But their practice cannot be found. {47}
{{milestone:{label:33.52,id:UT22084-055-001-3058}}}“Their passage cannot be found,
Like that of a bird through the sky.
The bodhisattvas realize
That nature of enlightenment. {48}
{{milestone:{label:33.53,id:UT22084-055-001-3059}}}“Just as a well-trained conjurer
Is able to display illusions,
Although there are many kinds of forms
There is no form that can be grasped. {49}
{{milestone:{label:33.54,id:UT22084-055-001-3060}}}“There is no pride in acquisition or nonacquisition,
As there is no acquisition in acquisition.
That wisdom is like an illusion,
And that illusion has no location. {50}
{{milestone:{label:33.55,id:UT22084-055-001-3061}}}“Thus the understanding of fools
Is a conceptualization of empty phenomena.
Engaging in conceptualization,
They are doomed to the six existences. {51}
{{milestone:{label:33.56,id:UT22084-055-001-3062}}}“Beings undergo rebirth and aging; 
There is no end to their being reborn.
There is no end to the suffering
Of skandhas that are born and die. {52}
{{milestone:{label:33.57,id:UT22084-055-001-3063}}}“The suffering of birth and saṃsāra
Is the conceptualization of foolish understanding.
This does not cease throughout eons;
Beings continue in saṃsāra for millions of eons. {53}
{{milestone:{label:33.58,id:UT22084-055-001-3064}}}“They continue in the performance of activities,
Whether that of engagement or disengagement.
They delight in the actions they perform,
But those activities will not liberate them. {54}
{{milestone:{label:33.59,id:UT22084-055-001-3065}}}“They are carried along on a river of actions,
And their actions will have no end.
They will die over and over,
Always dwelling in the realm of the māras. {55}
{{milestone:{label:33.60,id:UT22084-055-001-3066}}}“Overpowered by the māras, with poor understanding, 
They act through being afflicted by the kleśas.
They experience births and deaths
That take place in various worlds. {56}
{{milestone:{label:33.61,id:UT22084-055-001-3067}}}“Those various beings who are blind fools, 
They proceed toward death. 
They are killed and destroyed,
And their existences are terrible. {57}
{{milestone:{label:33.62,id:UT22084-055-001-3068}}}“Those with foolish understanding
Kill each other with weapons.
By continuing with that kind of activity
Their sufferings only increase. {58}
{{milestone:{label:33.63,id:UT22084-055-001-3069}}}“Those with foolish understanding think,
‘My sons’ and ‘my wealth.’ 
They conceive of that which has no existence
And thereby continue to extend saṃsāra. {59}
{{milestone:{label:33.64,id:UT22084-055-001-3070}}}“They who extend saṃsāra,
Those individuals continue in saṃsāra.
They each go their individual ways
And therefore they are called individual beings. {60}
{{milestone:{label:33.65,id:UT22084-055-001-3071}}}“They reject the Buddha’s teaching {{page:{number:211,id:UT22084-055-001-6044,folio:F.106.b}}}
And teach numerous other doctrines.
They are under the power of Māra
And they will not attain liberation. {61}
{{milestone:{label:33.66,id:UT22084-055-001-3072}}}“These fools, because of their desires, 
Have intercourse with putrid women.
They will be reborn as putrid beings,
Falling into the lower realms as a result. {62}
{{milestone:{label:33.67,id:UT22084-055-001-3073}}}“The buddhas praise neither desire,
Nor having intercourse with women. 
That is a terrifying noose,
The dreadful noose of women. {63}
{{milestone:{label:33.68,id:UT22084-055-001-3074}}}“Those who are wise avoid it
Like a vicious poisonous snake.
They do not put their trust in women.
That is not the path to enlightenment. {64}
{{milestone:{label:33.69,id:UT22084-055-001-3075}}}“They meditate on the path to enlightenment 
That has been taught{{note:{index1076,id:UT22084-055-001-3076}}} by all the buddhas.
Having meditated on that path
They become unsurpassable buddhas. {65}
{{milestone:{label:33.70,id:UT22084-055-001-3077}}}“Those who have become unsurpassable
Become shrines in the world.
With unsurpassable wisdom
They become unsurpassable buddhas. {66}
{{milestone:{label:33.71,id:UT22084-055-001-3078}}}“They follow the poṣadha vows
And follow the path of correct conduct.
They lead toward enlightenment 
Countless millions of beings. {67}
{{milestone:{label:33.72,id:UT22084-055-001-3079}}}“They accomplish the benefit of
Innumerable, countless beings.
They are heroes with great wisdom
Who beat the drum of deathlessness. {68}
{{milestone:{label:33.73,id:UT22084-055-001-3080}}}“They make the realm of Māra shudder;
They make the māras shake.
They lead to enlightenment
Countless millions of māras. {69}
{{milestone:{label:33.74,id:UT22084-055-001-3081}}}“They overcome their opponents.
They defeat the tīrthikas.
They shake the entire earth
With its mountains and oceans. {70}
{{milestone:{label:33.75,id:UT22084-055-001-3082}}}“The great leaders{{note:{index1077,id:UT22084-055-001-3083}}} through many transformations 
Manifest miraculous manifestations of the body.
The great wise ones display
Inconceivable miracles. {71}
{{milestone:{label:33.76,id:UT22084-055-001-3084}}}“They shake millions of realms
As numerous as the Ganges sands.
They defeat the māras
And are greatly famed buddhas.{{note:{index1078,id:UT22084-055-001-3085}}} {72}
{{milestone:{label:33.77,id:UT22084-055-001-3086}}}“They manifest trees{{note:{index1079,id:UT22084-055-001-3087}}}
Adorned with jewels,
Aromatic and beautiful,
Bearing flowers and fruits. {73}
{{milestone:{label:33.78,id:UT22084-055-001-3088}}}“Those heroes emanate
Delightful{{note:{index1080,id:UT22084-055-001-3089}}} mansions,{{note:{index1081,id:UT22084-055-001-3090}}}{{page:{number:212,id:UT22084-055-001-6045,folio:F.107.a}}}
Palaces and pinnacled halls,
And beautiful lotus ponds{{note:{index1082,id:UT22084-055-001-3091}}} {74}
{{milestone:{label:33.79,id:UT22084-055-001-3092}}}“Filled with water that has the eight qualities,
That is clear, cool, and unstained.
Those who drink that water
Cease yearning for the three existences. {75}
{{milestone:{label:33.80,id:UT22084-055-001-3093}}}“They become irreversible,
Those who drink that supreme water.
Through supreme wisdom
They become supreme buddhas. {76}
{{milestone:{label:33.81,id:UT22084-055-001-3094}}}“Know that they enter
The supreme way of peace.
Those who do not know that way,
Those focused on perceptions,{{note:{index1083,id:UT22084-055-001-3095}}} will perish. {77}
{{milestone:{label:33.82,id:UT22084-055-001-3096}}}“The beings who follow that way,
And those who depend upon them,
Will fall into the great terror
Of unendurable Avīci. {78}
{{milestone:{label:33.83,id:UT22084-055-001-3097}}}“The terrible sufferings there
Are beyond description,
But I and the bodhisattvas,
The protectors, know them. {79}
{{milestone:{label:33.84,id:UT22084-055-001-3098}}}“They doubt the Dharma,
Which is profound and difficult to see.
It is not on the level of fools,
Those who remain focused on perceptions. {80}
{{milestone:{label:33.85,id:UT22084-055-001-3099}}}“The manifestations of displays,
Of appearances of many forms,
They are all of them seen in 
The supreme buddha realms. {81}
{{milestone:{label:33.86,id:UT22084-055-001-3100}}}“All the appearances of manifested forms 
That are in every buddha realm 
Are all revealed here by bodhisattvas
With great miraculous powers. {82}
{{milestone:{label:33.87,id:UT22084-055-001-3101}}}“Those great heroes with great strength 
Wear the armor of the great Dharma.
They strike with the blows
Of the great vajra of the meaning of emptiness. {83}
{{milestone:{label:33.88,id:UT22084-055-001-3102}}}“Many thousands of millions of light rays
As numerous as the sands in the Ganges
Are radiated from their bodies
And they illuminate the world. {84}
{{milestone:{label:33.89,id:UT22084-055-001-3103}}}“They find no pleasure in women
And have no desire for them.
Those conceptions have been destroyed
Naturally with their conceptions of women. {85}
{{milestone:{label:33.90,id:UT22084-055-001-3104}}}“Wherever those heroes are present,
Those buddha realms are not empty.
How could the māras and evil ones
Create an obstacle for them? {86}
{{milestone:{label:33.91,id:UT22084-055-001-3105}}}“Those who remain in fabricated views
Displease a multitude of buddhas.
Those who are based upon maliciousness
Maintain their desires and attachments. {87}
{{milestone:{label:33.92,id:UT22084-055-001-3106}}}“All of those who maintain those views {{page:{number:213,id:UT22084-055-001-6046,folio:F.107.b}}}
Should be known to be māras.
But those māras and evil ones
Cannot cause them an obstacle.{{note:{index1084,id:UT22084-055-001-3107}}} {i}
{{milestone:{label:33.93,id:UT22084-055-001-3108}}}“When all conceptualization has ceased
They do not relapse into conceptualization.
That is how one should know wisdom to be,
The inconceivable wisdom of buddhahood. {88}
{{milestone:{label:33.94,id:UT22084-055-001-3109}}}“They see the past, the future,
And also the present.
Phenomena are revealed in that way, 
But there is nothing to be revealed. {89}
{{milestone:{label:33.95,id:UT22084-055-001-3110}}}“They do not know through knowledge.
They are not despondent because of no knowledge.
When knowledge and no knowledge have been examined
That is what is said to be ‘the knowledge of buddhahood.’{{note:{index1085,id:UT22084-055-001-3111}}} {90}
{{milestone:{label:33.96,id:UT22084-055-001-3112}}}“The bodhisattvas know
Communication, words, and terms,
And they accomplish immeasurable,
Inconceivable benefits for beings. {91}
{{milestone:{label:33.97,id:UT22084-055-001-3113}}}“In order for a concept to be known, 
It is taught through grasping.
The non-grasping of a concept
Is taught for the sake of detachment. {92}
{{milestone:{label:33.98,id:UT22084-055-001-3114}}}“That which is detachment is taught 
To be detachment from conceptions.{{note:{index1086,id:UT22084-055-001-3115}}}
As the nature of conceptions is known,{{note:{index1087,id:UT22084-055-001-3116}}}
There will be no{{note:{index1088,id:UT22084-055-001-3117}}} conceptions.{{note:{index1089,id:UT22084-055-001-3118}}} {93}
{{milestone:{label:33.99,id:UT22084-055-001-3119}}}“When someone has the conception
‘I must eliminate this conception,’
They cause conceptions to increase,
And they will not be free from conceptions. {94}
{{milestone:{label:33.100,id:UT22084-055-001-3120}}}“For whom has this conception arisen?
Who has made this conception arise?
Who perceives this conception?
Who ends this conception? {95}
{{milestone:{label:33.101,id:UT22084-055-001-3121}}}“When a conception arises for anyone,
Even a buddha could not find any such phenomenon.
Contemplate the meaning of this
And there will be no conception. {96}
{{milestone:{label:33.102,id:UT22084-055-001-3122}}}“When does a conception arise?
For whom does the conception appear? 
How does liberation arise
In the process of the mind? {97}
{{milestone:{label:33.103,id:UT22084-055-001-3123}}}“When liberation is experienced,
All thoughts become nonthought.
When thoughts become nonthought, 
At that time there is nonthought. {98}
{{milestone:{label:33.104,id:UT22084-055-001-3124}}}“When one is on the level of thoughts,
Having thus contemplated,
All thoughts are eliminated
And there is nonthought. {99}
{{milestone:{label:33.105,id:UT22084-055-001-3125}}}“This is the ripening of good qualities, {{page:{number:214,id:UT22084-055-001-6047,folio:F.108.a}}}
Which is seen without mentation,
And the thoughts of all beings
Are known in a single instant. {100}
{{milestone:{label:33.106,id:UT22084-055-001-3126}}}“As beings are, so are their thoughts;
As are their thoughts, so are the jinas.
The inconceivable Buddha
Has taught these thoughts. {101}
{{milestone:{label:33.107,id:UT22084-055-001-3127}}}“When will thoughts cease for those
Who think of being alone in solitude?
When they do not think that thought
Then all thoughts will cease to be. {102}
{{milestone:{label:33.108,id:UT22084-055-001-3128}}}“When it comes to the time of death
And their thoughts are continuing,
Their consciousness will follow the thoughts
And they will not be free from thought. {103}
{{milestone:{label:33.109,id:UT22084-055-001-3129}}}“If a man retains the concept of a woman,
His desire will continue to arise. 
If this concept has ceased
He will not be stained by desire. {104}
{{milestone:{label:33.110,id:UT22084-055-001-3130}}}“This thought is a great thought;
It is the unsurpassable thought of the Dharma.
Through this thought of the Dharma
There will be a continuity of correct thoughts. {105}
{{milestone:{label:33.111,id:UT22084-055-001-3131}}}“Through incorrect thought
There will be numerous, countless thoughts,
And though one thinks for a very long time
There will still be no cessation to thinking. {106}
{{milestone:{label:33.112,id:UT22084-055-001-3132}}}“When someone has the thought of a name,
In that cessation there is no wisdom.{{note:{index1090,id:UT22084-055-001-3133}}}
There is no cessation in the knowledge of a word—{{note:{index1091,id:UT22084-055-001-3134}}}
That is the nature of cessation. {107}
{{milestone:{label:33.113,id:UT22084-055-001-3135}}}“Through words, speech, and communication, 
Phenomena are taught using the term cessation.
Between phenomena there is no distinction,
And through knowing that there is cessation; {108}
{{milestone:{label:33.114,id:UT22084-055-001-3136}}}“Even if it is explained for ten million eons
That they are unproduced and unceasing,
Without attributes and without characteristics,
They are taught to be without attributes. {109}
{{milestone:{label:33.115,id:UT22084-055-001-3137}}}“When all existents have ceased to exist
And they remain in nonexistence,
Existence is not taught to be other than nonexistence,
And nonexistence is not taught to be other than existence. {110}
{{milestone:{label:33.116,id:UT22084-055-001-3138}}}“The teaching of nonexistence
Is given through the word nonexistence,
But not even all the buddhas
Can see nonexistence. {111}
{{milestone:{label:33.117,id:UT22084-055-001-3139}}}“That which exists is taught
As this nonexistence of all that exists.
Knowing existents in this way,
They are taught to be nonexistent. {112}
{{milestone:{label:33.118,id:UT22084-055-001-3140}}}“There is no one whosoever
Who can connect with this nonexistence.
The connection with this nonexistence
Results in a teaching that is one of conventions.{{note:{index1092,id:UT22084-055-001-3141}}} {113}
{{milestone:{label:33.119,id:UT22084-055-001-3142}}}“The ones who have in their minds the thought {{page:{number:215,id:UT22084-055-001-6048,folio:F.108.b}}}
‘I shall become a buddha in this world’
Will not be afflicted by craving for existence,
And those wise ones will attain enlightenment. {114}
{{milestone:{label:33.120,id:UT22084-055-001-3143}}}“The bodhisattvas in meditation
Do not long for any phenomenon.
When nothing is apprehended,{{note:{index1093,id:UT22084-055-001-3144}}}
That is called enlightenment. {115}
{{milestone:{label:33.121,id:UT22084-055-001-3145}}}“There are many who say, 
‘I am in a state of enlightenment,’
But not knowing this approach
They are far from buddhahood’s enlightenment. {116}
{{milestone:{label:33.122,id:UT22084-055-001-3146}}}“The Dharma that is taught through words
Is entirely composite and empty.
The nature of these words 
Is profound, subtle, and difficult to see. {117}
{{milestone:{label:33.123,id:UT22084-055-001-3147}}}“It is through great higher cognition 
That the teaching of this sūtra is given.
It is taught by all the buddhas 
For the sake of the bodhisattvas. {118}
{{milestone:{label:33.124,id:UT22084-055-001-3148}}}“Remedies defeat 
However many kleśas they have.
Remaining in higher cognition,
They cultivate miraculous powers. {119}
{{milestone:{label:33.125,id:UT22084-055-001-3149}}}“They maintain the knowledge of contemplation
And then that knowledge also ceases.
There is an insatiable acquisition 
Of inconceivable, immeasurable wisdom. {120}
{{milestone:{label:33.126,id:UT22084-055-001-3150}}}“Their samādhi and miraculous actions
Are devoid of mentation.
Such is the ripening of these heroes
Who are always in a state of meditation. {121}
{{milestone:{label:33.127,id:UT22084-055-001-3151}}}“With these ripened miraculous powers
They go to millions of realms
And they see those who are the illumination of the worlds,
Who are as numerous as the sands of the Ganges. {122}
{{milestone:{label:33.128,id:UT22084-055-001-3152}}}“Their births and their deaths
Are the processes of their minds.
They have attained power over their minds
And their bodies are bright. {123}
{{milestone:{label:33.129,id:UT22084-055-001-3153}}}“The Buddha’s śrāvakas who maintain
The miraculous powers they have cultivated 
Do not even approach a sixteenth fraction
Of the miraculous activities free of mentation. {124}
{{milestone:{label:33.130,id:UT22084-055-001-3154}}}“All the devas are unable
To know their thoughts.
Only the lords of the worlds,
And those who are equal to them, can do so. {125}
{{milestone:{label:33.131,id:UT22084-055-001-3155}}}“They do not become bald
And their hair does not become white.
They do not have evident aging
And thus have no suffering or death. {126}
{{milestone:{label:33.132,id:UT22084-055-001-3156}}}“They do not have doubt or mistrust
And they have no uncertainty. {{page:{number:216,id:UT22084-055-001-6049,folio:F.109.a}}}
Day and night they seek for
Thousands of millions of sūtras. {127}
{{milestone:{label:33.133,id:UT22084-055-001-3157}}}“All their propensities 
For the kleśas are eliminated.
They always have an equal mind
Toward all beings. {128}
{{milestone:{label:33.134,id:UT22084-055-001-3158}}}“They teach quintillions of samādhis
Throughout the ten directions.
Without respite they answer 
Thousand of millions of questions. {129}
{{milestone:{label:33.135,id:UT22084-055-001-3159}}}“The concept of male, the concept of female,
And all other concepts have ceased.
They remain in the recognition of nonexistence
And they teach that which is certain and true. {130}
{{milestone:{label:33.136,id:UT22084-055-001-3160}}}“With completely pure wisdom
They teach the Dharma correctly.
They are dedicated to proclaiming the Dharma,
And are in the domain of samādhi and wisdom. {131}
{{milestone:{label:33.137,id:UT22084-055-001-3161}}}“Though they practice dhyāna,
They do not remain in existence.
Their words are not meaningless;
Their teaching of the Dharma is fruitful. {132}
{{milestone:{label:33.138,id:UT22084-055-001-3162}}}“Those who delight in this sūtra
Will easily become human, 
Avoid all disadvantageous existences,
And repay the kindness of all the buddhas. {133}
{{milestone:{label:33.139,id:UT22084-055-001-3163}}}“Those who possess one verse
Of this precious sūtra
Will abandon saṃsāra
For countless eons. {134}
{{milestone:{label:33.140,id:UT22084-055-001-3164}}}“Those who delight in this sūtra
Are seen by all the buddhas.
They will serve the buddhas
And quickly attain enlightenment. {135}
{{milestone:{label:33.141,id:UT22084-055-001-3165}}}“Those who delight in this sūtra,
They will have no doubt or uncertainty
Concerning the entire Dharma,
And they are near to nirvāṇa. {136}
{{milestone:{label:33.142,id:UT22084-055-001-3166}}}“They will see a great hero,
A tathāgata on Gṛdhrakūṭa.
All the buddhas will give them prophecies 
And they will appear to be compassionate jinas. {137}
{{milestone:{label:33.143,id:UT22084-055-001-3167}}}“Those who follow this sūtra 
In this time of destruction
Will see Buddha Maitreya
And attain excellent patience. {138}
{{milestone:{label:33.144,id:UT22084-055-001-3168}}}“They will remain at the summit of existence,
The inconceivable summit of existence,
And at that inconceivable summit
They will know no doubt. {139}
{{milestone:{label:33.145,id:UT22084-055-001-3169}}}“They will not have any doubt at all,
Not even an atom of doubt.
As they have eliminated every atom of doubt,{{note:{index1094,id:UT22084-055-001-3170}}}
Enlightenment will not be difficult to attain. {140} {{page:{number:217,id:UT22084-055-001-6050,folio:F.109.b}}}
{{milestone:{label:33.146,id:UT22084-055-001-3171}}}“In the terrifying age of destruction
They will undergo hardship,
Train in this precious sūtra,
And have an unceasing eloquence.{{note:{index1095,id:UT22084-055-001-3172}}} {141}
{{milestone:{label:33.147,id:UT22084-055-001-3173}}}“They will promulgate this sūtra
And will guard the treasure of the buddhas.
This is an offering to all the buddhas,
An inconceivable offering of the Dharma. {142}
{{milestone:{label:33.148,id:UT22084-055-001-3174}}}“Those who maintain this sūtra
During the cruel age of destruction
Will without difficulty attain wisdom,
The inconceivable wisdom of buddhahood. {143}
{{milestone:{label:33.149,id:UT22084-055-001-3175}}}“Those who received this sūtra
From the buddhas of the past
Will come into possession of it
And promulgate it in the age of destruction. {144}
{{milestone:{label:33.150,id:UT22084-055-001-3176}}}“Their voices will proclaim
The conduct of the Śākya lion
In the presence of lords of the world
In millions of buddha realms. {145}
{{milestone:{label:33.151,id:UT22084-055-001-3177}}}“And in the presence of the buddhas{{note:{index1096,id:UT22084-055-001-3178}}}
They will always roar the lion’s roar
With an endless confidence of speech,
Teaching the enlightenment of buddhahood. {146}
{{milestone:{label:33.152,id:UT22084-055-001-3179}}}“Those who have been prophesied by the Buddha
Will be born into the Ikṣvāku family.
They will protect this enlightenment
During the terrifying age of destruction. {147}
{{milestone:{label:33.153,id:UT22084-055-001-3180}}}“Their bodies will be perfect,
Adorned by the primary signs of a great being.
They will send emanations 
To make homage to millions of buddhas. {148}
{{milestone:{label:33.154,id:UT22084-055-001-3181}}}“There will be the manifestation 
Of golden, illusory flowers, 
And flowers made of beryl, 
Of crystal, and of silver, {149}
{{milestone:{label:33.155,id:UT22084-055-001-3182}}}“And every kind of jewel
Appearing from their hands, 
Which they will scatter toward the buddhas
In seeking the path to enlightenment. {150}
{{milestone:{label:33.156,id:UT22084-055-001-3183}}}“Various kinds of offerings,
And perfectly created music,
As numerous as the Ganges sands,
Will be emitted from the pores of their bodies. {151}
{{milestone:{label:33.157,id:UT22084-055-001-3184}}}“The countless millions of beings
Who hear that music
Will progress irreversibly toward
Buddhahood’s highest wisdom. {152}
{{milestone:{label:33.158,id:UT22084-055-001-3185}}}“Those millions of buddhas
Recite countless praises
And their sound is heard
Within countless realms. {153}
{{milestone:{label:33.159,id:UT22084-055-001-3186}}}“For those who hear that sound
All their conceptualization ceases. {{page:{number:218,id:UT22084-055-001-6051,folio:F.110.a}}}
When their conceptualization has ceased
They will see endless{{note:{index1097,id:UT22084-055-001-3187}}} buddhas. {154}
{{milestone:{label:33.160,id:UT22084-055-001-3188}}}“With that kind of wisdom
They will practice bodhisattva conduct.
They will benefit all beings
And become jinas who benefit others. {155}
{{milestone:{label:33.161,id:UT22084-055-001-3189}}}“Those who possess this samādhi
Are wise ones who will obtain 
These benefits and qualities,
And also countless others. {156}
{{milestone:{label:33.162,id:UT22084-055-001-3190}}}“Even a female who hears
This sūtra and retains a single verse
Will change from having a female existence
And will become a dharmabhāṇaka. {157}
{{milestone:{label:33.163,id:UT22084-055-001-3191}}}“She will never again afterward 
Have a female existence,
And will always be handsome
And adorned by the primary signs of a great being. {158}
{{milestone:{label:33.164,id:UT22084-055-001-3192}}}“They will all come to possess
These supreme qualities 
Described in this supreme sūtra, 
And they will quickly attain enlightenment. {159}
{{milestone:{label:33.165,id:UT22084-055-001-3193}}}“Having obtained this sūtra,
Which is the domain of all the buddhas,{{note:{index1098,id:UT22084-055-001-3194}}}
Throughout all their lifetimes
They will always be without fear. {160}
{{milestone:{label:33.166,id:UT22084-055-001-3195}}}“Teaching this samādhi, this peace
Is the creation of bodhisattvas.
Whoever wishes to attain enlightenment 
Should give the teaching of this sūtra. {161}
{{milestone:{label:33.167,id:UT22084-055-001-3196}}}“They will be close to the lords of sages
And will be close to buddhahood’s enlightenment.
They will before long attain
This level of peace and meditation. {162}
{{milestone:{label:33.168,id:UT22084-055-001-3197}}}“The bodhisattvas, the heroes,
Always remain in this enlightenment.
They see millions of buddhas
As numerous as the Ganges sands. {163}
{{milestone:{label:33.169,id:UT22084-055-001-3198}}}“They will become cakravartin kings who rule the world,
